(define (domain exploration)

  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))

  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

  )

    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)

    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))

  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)

  )

    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharp-object - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharp-object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT

    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT

    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)

    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

            If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
            Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (on ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )

    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )

    :effect (heated ?o)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (on ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (on ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (on ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (on ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

  (:types
    receptacle object - thing

  )

    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (sliced ?co)
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handempty)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (switched-on ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CLOSEOBJECT
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handempty)))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (in ?o ?r) (handempty) (not (holding ?o)))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (switched-on ?o)
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)

    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
